
###Grants and Money

country_event = {	
	id = 99999999
	title = "Money injection"
	desc = "Upon discovering that no single person in the world has any money, they have all raided their grandparents stockings to get at those savings."
	
	trigger = {
		year = 1836
		tag = HAW
		NOT = { has_global_flag = money_injected }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Great!"
		
		set_global_flag = money_injected
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
			OR = {
			is_secondary_power = yes 
			is_greater_power = yes
			}
		  }
			treasury = 500000
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { civilized = yes }
			treasury = 50000
		}
	}
}


country_event = {

	
	id = 100000
	
	title = "Aid Requested"
	
	desc = "We have requested aid from foreign powers. We can only hope they respond kindly."
	
	is_triggered_only = yes	
	
	allow_multiple_instances = yes	

	option = {
	
		name = "It is out of our hands."

		any_country = {
		
			limit = {
			
				ai = no
			
				money = 1000000
		
			}
		
			country_event = {id = 100001 days = 0}
	
		}	
	
		ai_chance = {factor = 100} 
	
	}	

}


country_event = {
	
id = 100002
	
	title = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ Grants Aid"
	
	desc = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ has decided to give us aid on the order of thousands of pounds."
	
	allow_multiple_instances = yes		
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
	
		name = "Great!"
	
		ai_chance = {factor = 100} 
	
		FROM = { country_event = {id = 100013 days = 0}}	
	
		FROM = { country_event = {id = 100003 days = 0}}
	
	}

}


country_event = {

	id = 100004

	title = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ Grants Aid"

	desc = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ has decided to give us aid on the order of tens of thousands of pounds."

	allow_multiple_instances = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {

		name = "Great!"
	
		ai_chance = {factor = 100}
		 
FROM = {

		country_event = {id = 100003 days = 0}

		country_event = {id = 100005 days = 0}
			
		}
	
	}

}


country_event = {

	id = 100006

	title = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ Grants Aid"

	desc = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ has decided to give us aid on the order of hundereds of thousands of pounds."

	is_triggered_only = yes
	allow_multiple_instances = yes
		
	option = {
	
			name = "Great!"
			
	ai_chance = {factor = 100}
	 
		FROM = {
			country_event = {id = 100005 days = 0}
	
 
			country_event = {id = 100007 days = 0}

		}

	}

}

	id = 100008

	title = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ Grants Aid"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	desc = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ has decided to give us aid on the order of millions of pounds."
	
	allow_multiple_instances = yes

			name = "Great!"
	ai_chance = {factor = 100}

			country_event = {id = 100009 days = 0}

		}

	}

}

country_event = {

	is_triggered_only = yes
	id = 100001
	title = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ Requests Aid"
	desc = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ has asked we give them a grant. How much should we give?"
	allow_multiple_instances = yes
	option = {
	name = "Our money is better spent at home."
		FROM = { country_event = {id = 100010 days = 0} }
	
	}
	option = {
	name = "Thousands of Pounds"
	
		FROM = {
			country_event = {id = 100002 days = 0}
		
		}
		ai_chance = {factor = 100} 
	}
	
	option = {
	name = "Tens of Thousands of Pounds"
	
		FROM = {
			country_event = {id = 100004 days = 0}
		} 
	}
	
	option = {
	name = "Hundreds of Thousands of Pounds"
	
		FROM = {
			country_event = {id = 100006 days = 0}
		} 
	}
	option = {
	name = "Millions of Pounds"
	
		FROM = {
			country_event = {id = 100008 days = 0}
		}
	}	
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	id = 100003
	title = "Choose Aid for $FROMCOUNTRY$"
	desc = "How much money would you like to give $FROMCOUNTRY$ (thousands)?"

	}

	}
}

########NaturalDisasters#########

#Tunguska Meteor Strike
country_event = {
	id = 21500
	title = "EVTNAME21500"
	desc = "EVTDESC21500"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC21500_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC21500_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC21500_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "destroyed_forest"
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	major = yes
	
	trigger = {
	    tag = RUS
		year = 1908
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 4
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA21500"
		2694 = {
			any_pop = {
				reduce_pop = 0.10
			}
			life_rating = -10
		}
	}
}

#Krakatoa Explodes
country_event = {
	id = 21510
	title = "EVTNAME21510"
	desc = "EVTDESC21510"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC21510_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC21510_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC21510_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "pelee"
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	major = yes
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		year = 1883
		owns = 1414
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 5
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA21510"
		1414 = {
			any_pop = {
				reduce_pop = 0.1
			}
			life_rating = -10
		}
	}
}

# 880270 - Train Accident Goods
country_event = {
	id = 880270
	title = "EVTNAME880270"
	desc = "EVTDESC880270"
	picture = "trainwreck"
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		NOT = {	has_country_modifier = national_tragedy }
		invention = industrial_railroads
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 900		  
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			invention = the_iron_horse
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			invention = commercial_railroads
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			invention = arteries_of_commerce
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			invention = autobahn
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			safety_regulations = no_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			safety_regulations = trinket_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			safety_regulations = low_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			safety_regulations = acceptable_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3.0
			safety_regulations = good_safety
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Horrible!"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = national_tragedy
			duration = 730
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				location = { is_colonial = no }
				country = {
					safety_regulations = no_safety
				}
			}
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = trinket_safety
			}
		}
		any_pop = {	
			limit = {
				location = { is_colonial = no }
				country = {
					safety_regulations = trinket_safety
				}
			}
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = low_safety
			}
		}
			
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				location = { is_colonial = no }
				country = {
					safety_regulations = low_safety
				}
			}
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = acceptable_safety
			}
		}
			
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				location = { is_colonial = no }
				country = {
					safety_regulations = acceptable_safety
				}
			}
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = good_safety
			}
		}
	}
}

# 880280 - Train Accident Soldiers
country_event = {
	id = 880280
	title = "EVTNAME880280"
	desc = "EVTDESC880280"
	picture = "trainwreck"
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		NOT = {	has_country_modifier = national_tragedy }
		invention = railroad_transport_groups
		war = yes
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 900
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			war_exhaustion = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			war_exhaustion = 20
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			war_exhaustion = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			war_exhaustion = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			war_exhaustion = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			war_exhaustion = 75
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			safety_regulations = no_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			safety_regulations = trinket_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			safety_regulations = low_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			safety_regulations = acceptable_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3.0
			safety_regulations = good_safety
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Tell the truth."	
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = national_tragedy
			duration = 730
		}
		soldiers = {
			consciousness = 2
			militancy = 2
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				location = { is_colonial = no }
				country = {
					safety_regulations = no_safety
				}
			}
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = trinket_safety
			}
		}
		any_pop = {	
			limit = {
				location = { is_colonial = no }
				country = {
					safety_regulations = trinket_safety
				}
			}
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = low_safety
			}
		}
			
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				location = { is_colonial = no }
				country = {
					safety_regulations = low_safety
				}
			}
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = acceptable_safety
			}
		}
			
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				location = { is_colonial = no }
				country = {
					safety_regulations = acceptable_safety
				}
			}
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = good_safety
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Blame the enemy."
		prestige = -5		
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = national_tragedy
			duration = 730
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_primary_culture = yes
					is_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.10
				value = jingoism
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = anti_military
				factor = 2
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = pacifism
				factor = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

# 880290 - Airplane Crash!
country_event = {
	id = 880290
	title = "EVTNAME880290"
	desc = "EVTDESC880290"
	picture = "cholera" #Was not able to find a decent historical picture without clear (c) status. -GAGA
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		NOT = {	has_country_modifier = national_tragedy }
		#invention = commercial_aeronautics #does not exist, suggested by me. -GAGA
		invention = wright_n_langleys_aeroplanes
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 900
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			safety_regulations = no_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			safety_regulations = trinket_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			safety_regulations = low_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			safety_regulations = acceptable_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3.0
			safety_regulations = good_safety
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "We will consider it."	
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = national_tragedy
			duration = 730
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				location = { is_colonial = no }
				country = {
					safety_regulations = no_safety
				}
			}
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = trinket_safety
			}
		}
		any_pop = {	
			limit = {
				location = { is_colonial = no }
				country = {
					safety_regulations = trinket_safety
				}
			}
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = low_safety
			}
		}
			
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				location = { is_colonial = no }
				country = {
					safety_regulations = low_safety
				}
			}
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = acceptable_safety
			}
		}
			
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				location = { is_colonial = no }
				country = {
					safety_regulations = acceptable_safety
				}
			}
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = good_safety
			}
		}
	}
}

# 880300 - Zeppelin Explodes!
country_event = {
	id = 880300
	title = "EVTNAME880300"
	desc = "EVTDESC880300"
	picture = "hindenburg" #Added by me, taken from wikipedia, no (c). -GAGA
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		NOT = {	has_country_modifier = national_tragedy }
		#invention = airships_and_zeppelins #does not exist, suggested by me. -GAGA
		invention = wright_n_langleys_aeroplanes
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 900
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			safety_regulations = no_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			safety_regulations = trinket_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			safety_regulations = low_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			safety_regulations = acceptable_safety
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3.0
			safety_regulations = good_safety
		}
	}
	
	option = {

		prestige = -5	
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = national_tragedy
			duration = 730
		}
		any_pop = {

				country = {
					safety_regulations = no_safety
				}
			}
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = trinket_safety
			}
		}
		any_pop = {

				location = { is_colonial = no }
				country = {
					safety_regulations = trinket_safety
				}
			}

				factor = 0.05

			}

## Discovery of the Source of the Nile
country_event = {

	id =  23200 # First attempt

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		not = { has_global_flag = NileDiscovered }
		not = { has_country_flag = NoGoToNile }
		not = { has_country_flag = YesGoToNileAgain }
		not = { has_country_flag = YesGoToNile }
		not = { has_country_flag = YesGoToNileThird }
		not = { owns = 2019 } # Entebbe, where direct source of Nile is located
		is_greater_power = yes # Nation is a great power
		year = 1866 # Will happen sometime after 1866
	}

	mean_time_to_happen =  {
		months = 12

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			year = 1870
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			year = 1875
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			year = 1880
		}
	}

	title = "EVTNAME23200"
	desc = "EVTDESC23200"
	picture = "Nile"
	

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA23200" # Support the mission
		money = -100000
		set_country_flag = YesGoToNile
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { money = 100000 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB23200" # Consider the idea later
		prestige = -5
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 45
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC23200" # Reject the idea
		set_country_flag = NoGoToNile
		prestige = -10
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
	}
}

## Discovery of the South Pole
country_event = {

	id = 23208 # First attempt

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		not = { has_global_flag = SouthPoleDiscovered }
		not = { has_country_flag = NoGoToSouthPole }
		not = { has_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPoleAgain }
		not = { has_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPole }
		not = { has_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPoleThird }
		is_greater_power = yes # Nation is a great power
		year = 1906 # Will happen sometime after 1906
	}

	mean_time_to_happen =  {
		months = 12

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			year = 1908
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			year = 1910
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			year = 1912
		}
	}

	title = "EVTNAME23208"
	desc = "EVTDESC23208"
	picture = "SouthPole1"

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA23200" # Support the mission
		money = -100000
		set_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPole
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { money = 100000 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB23200" # Consider the idea later
		ai_chance = { factor = 45 }
		prestige = -5
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC23208" # Reject the idea
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		set_country_flag = NoGoToSouthPole
		prestige = -10
	}
}

country_event = {

	id = 23209 # First attempt fails, try again?

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		has_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPole
		not = { has_global_flag = SouthPoleDiscovered }
		not = { has_country_flag = NoGoToSouthPole }
		year = 1908 # Will happen sometime after 1908
	}

	mean_time_to_happen =  {
		months = 12

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			year = 1909
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			year = 1910
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			year = 1911
		}
	}

	title = "EVTNAME23201"
	desc = "EVTDESC23209"
	picture = "SouthPole2"

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA23201" # Fund second attempt
		money = -200000
		set_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPoleAgain
		clr_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPole
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { money = 200000 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB23201" # Reject second attempt
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		clr_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPole
		set_country_flag = NoGoToSouthPole
		prestige = -5
	}
}

country_event = {

	id = 23210 # Our Mission to the South Pole is lost

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		has_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPoleAgain
		not = { has_global_flag = SouthPoleDiscovered }
		not = { has_country_flag = NoGoToSouthPole }
		year = 1910 # Will happen sometime after 1910
	}

	mean_time_to_happen =  {
		months = 24

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			year = 1911
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			year = 1912
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			year = 1913
		}
	}

	title = "EVTNAME23202"
	desc = "EVTDESC23210"
	picture = "SouthPole2"

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA23201" # Fund third attempt
		money = -200000
		set_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPoleThird
		set_country_flag = expedition_fail_south
		set_global_flag = expedition_fail_south_global
		clr_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPoleAgain
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { money = 200000 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB23201" # Reject second attempt
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		clr_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPoleAgain
		set_country_flag = NoGoToSouthPole
		set_country_flag = expedition_fail_south
		set_global_flag = expedition_fail_south_global
		prestige = -5
	}
}

country_event = {

	id = 23211 # The South Pole is discovered!
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC23211_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC23211_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC23211_NEWS_SHORT"

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		or = {
			has_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPoleAgain
			has_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPoleThird
		}
		not = { has_global_flag = SouthPoleDiscovered }
		not = { has_country_flag = NoGoToSouthPole }
		year = 1910 # Will happen sometime after 1910
	}
	major = yes
	mean_time_to_happen =  {
		months = 12

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			year = 1912
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			year = 1913
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			year = 1914
		}
	}

	title = "EVTNAME23211"
	desc = "EVTDESC23211"
	picture = "SouthPole3"

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA23203" # Success!
		prestige = 25
		set_global_flag = SouthPoleDiscovered
		set_country_flag = has_discovered_the_south_pole
		clr_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPoleAgain
		clr_country_flag = YesGoToSouthPoleThird
	}
}

#############Archaeology#########
country_event = {
	id = 190401
	title = "Mycenaean Excavations"
	desc = "A great power has come to us asking to excavate local ruins."
	picture = "ValleyoftheKings"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Certainly"
		set_global_flag = greek_excavation_rights
		FROM = {
			country_event = 190411
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_global_flag = greek_excavation_rights
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				FROM = {
					prestige = 365
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = {
					is_greater_power = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Never!"
		FROM = {
			country_event = 190421
		}
	}
}

#Egypt Allows
country_event = {
	id = 190411
	title = "Greece permits!"
	desc = "The Greeks have agreed that we may excavate at Mycenae"
	picture = "ValleyoftheKings"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Hurrah!"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = mycenaean_excavations
			duration = -1
		}
		relation = {
			who = FROM
			value = 20
		}
		set_global_flag = mycenaean_excavation_rights
		prestige = 5
	}
}

#Egypt Refuses
country_event = {
	id = 190421
	title = "Greece refuses!"
	desc = "The foolish Greeks have refused our antiquarians access!"
	picture = "ValleyoftheKings"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Damnation!"
		relation = {
			who = FROM
			value = -20
		}
		prestige = -5
		set_country_flag = greece_refused
	}
}

# Excavation team gets into trouble
country_event = {
	id = 190431
	title = "Legal Issues"
	desc = "There's been some unfortunate allegations in Greece..."
	picture = "ValleyoftheKings"
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		has_country_modifier = mycenaean_excavations
		NOT = {
			owns = 840
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "A little money may help?"
		treasury = -20000
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { money = 20000 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Bring them home"
		relation = {
			who = GRE
			value = -20
		}
		clr_global_flag = mycenaean_excavation_rights
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 190461
	title = "The Face of Agamemnon"
	desc = "And as we pulled the mask from the body, I gazed into the face of Agamemnon."
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC190461_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC190461_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC190461_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "Egyptian"	
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		has_country_modifier = mycenaean_excavations
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = agamemnon_found
		}
	}
	
	major = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Splendid"
		prestige = 15
		years_of_research = 1
		set_global_flag = agamemnon_found
		any_country = {
			remove_country_modifier = mycenaean_excavations
		}
		remove_country_modifier = mycenaean_excavations
		clr_global_flag = mycenaean_excavation_rights
	}
}

##Crime####
# Trustee System
country_event = {
	id = 22000
	title = "EVTNAME22000"
	desc = "EVTDESC22000"
	picture = "prisonworkers"

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		crime_fighting = 0.5
		civilized = yes
		NOT = {
			poor_strata_everyday_needs = 0.8
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_modifier = trustee_system
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			average_militancy = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			average_militancy = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			average_militancy = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_consciousness = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_consciousness = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_consciousness = 7
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = {	average_militancy = 3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { average_consciousness = 2 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			social_science = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA22000"
		random_state = {
			any_owned = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = trustee_system
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB22000"
		random_state = {
			any_pop = {
				consciousness = 2
				militancy = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

# Penal Colony
country_event = {
	id = 22010
	title = "EVTNAME22010"
	desc = "EVTDESC22010"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC22010_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC22010_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC22010_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "penal_colony"
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		civilized = yes
		any_owned_province = {
			is_colonial = yes
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = penal_colonies
			poor_strata_everyday_needs = 0.9
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 400
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			crime_fighting = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			crime_fighting = 0.6
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			crime_fighting = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			crime_fighting = 0.8
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			crime_fighting = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_militancy = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_militancy = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_militancy = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_consciousness = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_consciousness = 6
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_consciousness = 9
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			poor_strata_life_needs = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			NOT = { poor_strata_life_needs = 0.9 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA22010"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = penal_colonies
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB22010"
		any_pop = {
			militancy = -0.5
		}
	}
}

# Penal Reform League
country_event = {
	id = 22020
	title = "EVTNAME22020"
	desc = "EVTDESC22020"
	picture = "prisoners"
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		civilized = yes
		NOT = {
			poor_strata_everyday_needs = 0.9
		}
		average_militancy = 2
		state_n_government = 1
		liberal = 0.1
	}

province_event = {
	
	id = 97100
	title = "EVTNAME97100" #Rebellion in Indian State
	desc = "EVTDESC97100"
	
	trigger = {
		is_core = HND
		controlled_by = THIS
		OR = {
			culture = bengali
			culture = nepali
			culture = panjabi
			culture = kashmiri
			culture = marathi
			culture = sindi
		}
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = nationalist_agitation }
		owner = {
			NOT = { is_culture_group = south_asian }
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = sepoy_rebellion
				has_global_flag = indian_call_to_union
			}
		}
		NOT = { poor_strata_everyday_needs = 0.9 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 500
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			any_neighbor_province = {
				is_core = HND
				has_province_modifier = nationalist_agitation
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_neighbor_province = {
				is_core = HND
				controlled_by = REB
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			poor_strata_everyday_needs = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			poor_strata_luxury_needs = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			NOT = { poor_strata_everyday_needs = 0.5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			NOT = { poor_strata_everyday_needs = 0.3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			NOT = { poor_strata_everyday_needs = 0.1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			NOT = { poor_strata_life_needs = 0.8 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { average_consciousness = 3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			owner = { war = yes }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Unacceptable!"
		state_scope = {
			any_pop = {
				limit = {
					is_culture_group = south_asian
					location = { is_core = HND }

			}

				limit = {
					is_core = HND

						culture = bengali

						culture = marathi
						culture = sindi
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = nationalist_agitation
					duration = 365
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = 97116

	desc = "EVTDESC97116"

	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC97116_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC97116_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "ranjit_singh_death"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Instability in the Panjab is unacceptable."
		relation = { who = PNJ value = -300 }
		leave_alliance = PNJ
		war = {
			target = PNJ
			attacker_goal = { casus_belli = conquest_any }
			defender_goal = { casus_belli = status_quo }
			call_ally = yes
			}
		ai_chance = {

#Nationalist Agitation
province_event = {
	id = 15315
	title = "EVTNAME15315"
	desc = "EVTDESC15315"
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = nationalist_agitation }
		is_primary_culture = no
		is_accepted_culture = no
		controlled_by = owner
		any_core = {
			is_cultural_union = no
			exists = no
			NOT = { is_primary_culture = THIS }
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = nationalist_agitation }
				}
				separatist = 25
			}
			AND = {
				any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = nationalist_agitation }
				separatist = 15
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { has_country_flag = liberal_revolution_in_progress }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = nationalist_agitation }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = nationalist_agitation }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { average_militancy = 1 }
			NOT = { average_consciousness = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { owner = { nationalism_n_imperialism = 1 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = the_age_of_nationalism } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_militancy = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_militancy = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_militancy = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_militancy = 6
		}
	}

					value = separatist
					factor = 0.10
				}
			}
		}
	}

	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC1000_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC1000_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "Socialism"
	
	trigger = {	
		exists = yes
		NOT = {
			is_ideology_enabled = socialist 
		}
		has_country_flag = had_liberal_revolution
		or = {
			invention = pierre_joseph_proudhon
			invention = karl_marx
			invention = friedrich_engels
		}
	}
	major = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			poor_strata_life_needs = 0.95
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			not = { invention = karl_marx }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			not = { invention = friedrich_engels }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1000"
		enable_ideology = socialist
		prestige = 20
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				is_primary_culture = yes
				location = {
					is_colonial = no
				}
			}
			ideology = {

			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { num_of_cities = 10 }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					any_pop = {
						limit = {
							is_primary_culture = yes
							location = {
								is_colonial = no
							}
						}

							value = socialist

						}

#Mobilization during peace time ends in pops pissed
country_event = {
	id = 443034
	title = "EVTNAME443034"
	desc = "EVTDESC443034"
	picture = "conscription_marching"
	
	trigger = {
		is_mobilised = yes
		war = no
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = peacetime_mobilization }
		ai = no
		military_score = 5
		OR = {
			military_score = 10
			NOT = { any_core = { country_units_in_province = REB } }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6
		
		modifier = { factor = 1.5 is_secondary_power = yes is_greater_power = no }
		modifier = { factor = 2 is_secondary_power = no is_greater_power = no }
		modifier = { factor = 0.5 constructing_cb_progress = 0.1 }
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { badboy = 0.5 }
			any_neighbor_country = { NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } } casus_belli = THIS }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVT443034OPTA"
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { is_greater_power = yes } }
			owner = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = peacetime_mobilization duration = 365 }
	
			war_exhaustion = 10
			any_pop = { dominant_issue = { value = pacifism factor = 0.1 } }
		
			any_country = {
				limit = { neighbour = THIS NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } alliance_with = THIS casus_belli = THIS in_sphere = THIS } }
				casus_belli = { target = THIS type = cut_down_to_size months = 12 }
			}

			any_country = { limit = { is_greater_power = yes } relation = { who = THIS value = -75 } }
			any_country = { limit = { is_secondary_power = yes } relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } }
		
			any_country = {
				limit = { neighbour = THIS NOT = { vassal_of = THIS } NOT = { in_sphere = THIS } NOT = { alliance_with = THIS } }
					any_pop = { dominant_issue = { value = jingoism factor = 0.05 } }
					relation = { who = THIS value = -100 }
			}
		
			any_country = {
				limit = { neighbour = THIS NOT = { vassal_of = THIS } alliance_with = THIS }
					any_pop = { dominant_issue = { value = jingoism factor = 0.05 } }
					relation = { who = THIS value = -25 }
					}
				}
			}
		
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { is_greater_power = no is_secondary_power = yes } }
			owner = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = peacetime_mobilization duration = 365 }
	
			war_exhaustion = 10
			any_pop = { dominant_issue = { value = pacifism factor = 0.1 } }
			
			any_country = {
				limit = { neighbour = THIS NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } alliance_with = THIS casus_belli = THIS } }
				casus_belli = { target = THIS type = cut_down_to_size months = 12 }
			}
		
			any_country = { limit = { is_greater_power = yes } relation = { who = THIS value = -25 } }
		
		any_country = {
			limit = { neighbour = THIS NOT = { vassal_of = THIS } NOT = { alliance_with = THIS } }
				any_pop = { dominant_issue = { value = jingoism factor = 0.05 } }
				relation = { who = THIS value = -75 }
		}
		
		any_country = {
			limit = { neighbour = THIS NOT = { vassal_of = THIS } alliance_with = THIS }
				any_pop = { dominant_issue = { value = jingoism factor = 0.05 } }
				relation = { who = THIS value = -25 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { is_greater_power = no is_secondary_power = no } }
			owner = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = peacetime_mobilization duration = 182 }

#A House Divided
country_event = {
	id = 16000
	title = "EVTNAME16000"
	desc = "EVTDESC16000"
	major = yes
	
	trigger = {	
		tag = USA
		NOT = { has_global_flag = ACW_preparations }
		year = 1858
		OR = {
			AND = {
				slavery = yes_slavery
				NOT = { has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened }
				has_country_flag = john_browns_raid
				has_country_flag = dred_scott_decision
				OR = {
					upper_house = {
						ideology = liberal
						value = 0.35
					}
					AND = { 
						ruling_party_ideology = liberal
						year = 1854 
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				slavery = no_slavery
				NOT = { has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12
	}
	
	immediate = {
		USA = { 
			clr_country_flag = the_slavery_debate
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = usa_draft
				duration = -1
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = no_more_war

				name = neutrality
				duration = 30

			}

				name = no_more_war
				duration = 30
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = neutrality
				duration = 30
			}
		}

#End mobilisation pool bonus from civil war
country_event = {
	id = 16003
	title = "End of the War"
	desc = "With the war over, former soldiers are now returning home."
	picture = "Recruits"

	trigger = {	
		OR = {
			tag = USA
			tag = CSA
		}
		has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened
		war = no
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = usa_draft
			has_country_modifier = csa_draft
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "We thank them for their service."
		remove_country_modifier = usa_draft
		remove_country_modifier = csa_draft
		any_pop = {
			militancy = -1
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 16001
	title = "EVTNAME16001"
	desc = "EVTDESC16001"
	news = yes
	news_title = "EVTNAME16001_NEWS_TITLE"
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC16001_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC16001_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC16001_NEWS_SHORT"
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = "Slaves"
	
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		slavery = yes_slavery
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = american_civil_was_has_happened
			has_country_flag = house_gag_rule_enacted
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 20
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			NOT = {
				year = 1845
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			year = 1845
			NOT = {
				year = 1850
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
				year = 1860
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA16001"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = the_slavery_debate
			duration = 10950
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 16002
	title = "Gag Rule under scrutiny!"
	desc = "There is a significant element in the House of Representatives seeking to repeal the gag rule."
	picture = "Slaves"
	
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		slavery = yes_slavery
		has_country_flag = house_gag_rule_enacted
		upper_house = {
						ideology = liberal
						value = 0.1
					}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = american_civil_was_has_happened
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 50
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Repeal the gag rule"
		set_country_flag = house_gag_rule_repealed
		clr_country_flag = house_gag_rule_enacted
			any_state = {
				limit = {
					is_slave = yes
				}
				any_pop = {
					consciousness = 2
				}
			}		
	}
	option = {
		name = "No abolutionist nonsense for us!"
			any_state = {
				limit = {
					is_slave = no
				}
				any_pop = {
					consciousness = 2
				}
			}
	}
}

#Knights of The Golden Circle
province_event = {
	id = 16090
	title = "EVTNAME16090"
	desc = "EVTDESC16090"
	
	
	trigger = {
		owner = {
			tag = USA
			slavery = yes_slavery
		}
		state_scope = {
			is_colonial = no
		}
		any_neighbor_province = {
			state_scope = {
				is_slave = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened
			has_province_modifier = knights_of_the_golden_circle
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 2400
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_consciousness = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_consciousness = 6
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			NOT = {
				average_consciousness = 5
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA16090"
		state_scope = {
			any_owned = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = knights_of_the_golden_circle
					duration = 365
				}
			}
			any_pop = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { type = slaves }
				}
				dominant_issue = {
					value = yes_slavery
					factor = 0.05
				}
				ideology = {
					value = reactionary
					factor = 0.10
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB16090"
		state_scope = {
			any_pop = {
				consciousness = 1.5
			}
		}
	}
}

			has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened
			has_province_modifier = free_staters
		}
		any_neighbor_province = {
			state_scope = { 
				OR = { 
					is_slave = no
					is_colonial = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			has_province_modifier = border_ruffians
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = {
				has_country_flag = emigrant_aid_company
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA16180"
		state_scope = {
			any_owned = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = free_staters
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
			any_pop = {

		continent = north_america
		NOT = { is_core = CSA }
		OR = {
	        state_id = 131
			state_id = 133
			state_id = 105
			state_id = 100
			state_id = 132		
			state_id = 2149
			state_id = 2142
			state_id = 2138
			state_id = 2151
			state_id = 2159
			state_id = 2183
			state_id = 2161
			state_id = 2170
			state_id = 2172
			state_id = 2181
            state_id = 139
            state_id = 29
            state_id = 144
            state_id = 194	
            state_id = 188
            state_id = 185
            state_id = 218
            state_id = 211
            state_id = 2556
            state_id = 205
            state_id = 201
            state_id = 200	
            state_id = 196
		}
		owner = {
			tag = USA
			slavery = yes_slavery
			has_country_flag = hasmanifestdestiny
			NOT = { has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened }
		}
		OR = {
			average_consciousness = 6
			AND = {
			owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal }
				average_consciousness = 3
				}
			AND = {
				owner = { upper_house = { ideology = liberal value = 0.4 } }
				average_consciousness = 3
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			yes_slavery = 15
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			average_consciousness = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			average_consciousness = 5
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA16250"
		state_scope = { any_owned = { add_core = CSA }
			any_pop = {
				dominant_issue = {
					value = yes_slavery
					factor = 0.2
				}
				militancy = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 16300
	title = "EVTNAME16300"
	desc = "EVTDESC16300"
	picture = "Uncletom"
	
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		slavery = yes_slavery
		year = 1852
		NOT = { has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened }
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 4
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA16300"

		any_state = {
			limit = {
				is_slave = no
				is_colonial = no
			}
			any_pop = {
			consciousness = 2
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = no_slavery
			}
			ideology = {
				value = liberal
				factor = 0.05
			}	
			}
			
		}

		any_state = {
			limit = {
				is_slave = yes
				is_colonial = no
			}
			any_pop = {
				limit = { NOT = { type = slaves } }
			consciousness = 2
			
			dominant_issue = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = yes_slavery
			}
			
			ideology = {
				value = conservative
				factor = 0.05
			}	
	           }
			
		}
	}
}

#Mexican-American War
country_event = {
	id = 44126
	title = "EVTNAME44126" #USA Demands Northwest Territories!
	desc = "EVTDESC44126"
	picture = "treaty"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "No. That land is rightfully ours."
		set_country_flag = mexico_refused_usa_once
		USA = { country_event = 44127 }
		any_pop = {
			militancy = -1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "We cannot afford for this to escalate."
		set_country_flag = treaty_of_guadalupe_hidalgo
		all_core = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					region = TEX_132
					region = MEX_103
					region = MEX_94
					region = MEX_97
					region = MEX_85
					region = MEX_100
				}
			}
			remove_core = MEX
		}
		prestige = -20
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core = USA
					region = TEX_132
					region = MEX_103
					region = MEX_94
					region = MEX_97
					region = MEX_85
					region = MEX_100
					region = USA_106
					region = USA_129
				}
			}
			secede_province = USA
		}
		MEX = { money = 100000 }
		USA = {
			country_event = 44128
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_greater_power = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { in_sphere = USA }
				part_of_sphere = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				USA = { brigades_compare = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = {
					USA = { brigades_compare = 1 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				war_policy = jingoism
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = "Our military could use the target practice."

		diplomatic_influence = { who = MEX value = -200 }
		leave_alliance = MEX

			limit = {
				owner = { ai = yes }
			}
			owner = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = usa_draft

				}

		}

		}

			factor = 100
		}
	}

		name = "We don't need this to come to a war yet."

		any_pop = {

			militancy = 1

			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

	id = 87603

	desc = "With the end of slavery, most of the ex-slave states have enacted segregationist laws."
	picture = "dixie"

		tag = USA
		slavery = no_slavery
		has_global_flag = american_civil_war_has_happened
		any_owned_province = {
			is_core = CSA
		}
		NOT = {
			exists = CSA
			has_country_flag = jim_crow_laws
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 120
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5 #increase likelihood to happen
			has_country_flag = kkk
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5 #increase likelihood to happen
			year = 1876
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA16415"
		set_country_flag = jim_crow_laws
		any_owned = {
			limit = { is_core = CSA }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = jim_crow
				duration = -1
			}
			any_pop = {
				limit = { has_pop_culture = dixie }
				ideology = {
					value = conservative
					factor = 0.40
				}
				ideology = {
					value = reactionary
					factor = 0.20
				}			
				militancy = -2
				consciousness = -4
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	
	id = 1100130
	title = "End of the Recruitment Drive"
	desc = "Our recruitment drive has been a success and our efforts to recruit new soldiers is ending."
	picture = "greatwar"

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		has_country_flag = recruitment_drive
		OR = {
			AND = {
				war_policy = jingoism
				soldiers = 0.02
			}
			AND = {
				war_policy = pro_military
				soldiers = 0.015
			}
			AND = {
				war_policy = anti_military
				soldiers = 0.01
			}
			AND = {
				war_policy = pacifism
				soldiers = 0.005
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Excellent!"
		clr_country_flag = recruitment_drive
		remove_country_modifier = recruitment_drive
	}
}

	id = 1100131
	title = "The Recruitment Drive Continues"
	desc = "Our recruitment drive has been ongoing, yet still we aren't at the levels of potential recruits that we need."
	picture = "greatwar"

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = recruitment_drive }
		has_country_flag = recruitment_drive
		OR = {
			AND = {
				war_policy = jingoism
				NOT = { soldiers = 0.02 }
			}
			AND = {
				war_policy = pro_military
				NOT = { soldiers = 0.015 }
			}
			AND = {
				war_policy = anti_military
				NOT = { soldiers = 0.01 }
			}
			AND = {
				war_policy = pacifism
				NOT = { soldiers = 0.005 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "The recruitment must contiue."
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = recruitment_drive
			duration = 1825
		}
		any_pop = {
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = pacifism
				factor = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	
	id = 1100145
	title = "Army Recruitment Drive"
	desc = "Our levels of soldier recruitment are perilously low. Perhaps a concerted effort to bring recruits to the army is required?"
	picture = "greatwar"
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		ai = yes
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = recruitment_drive }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = recruitment_drive }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				war_policy = jingoism
				NOT = { soldiers = 0.02 }
			}
			AND = {
				war_policy = pro_military
				NOT = { soldiers = 0.015 }
			}
			AND = {
				war_policy = anti_military
				NOT = { soldiers = 0.01 }
			}
			AND = {
				war_policy = pacifism
				NOT = { soldiers = 0.005 }
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
			recruited_percentage = 0.75
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			NOT = { total_amount_of_divisions = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Begin the recruitment!"
		set_country_flag = recruitment_drive
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = recruitment_drive
			duration = 1825
		}
		any_pop = {
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = pacifism
				factor = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = "unite"
	fire_only_once = yes
	major = yes
	trigger = {	
	    exists = yes

	}

		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Raise the $COUNTRY_ADJ$ flag!"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = workshop_of_the_world
			duration = -1
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = workshop_of_the_world
					NOT = { tag = THIS }
			}
			country_event = 1100144
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 11380019
	title = "EVTNAME11380019" #Constitutional Crisis - Fascists in HMS Government
	desc = "EVTDESC11380019"
	news = yes
	news_title = "EVTNAME11380019_NEWS_TITLE"
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC11380019_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC11380019_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC11380019_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "Bankruptcy"
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		government = hms_government
		ruling_party_ideology = fascist
		NOT = { has_country_flag = political_showdown }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { ai = no }
			}
			owner = { set_country_flag = political_showdown }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "This cannot be allowed. The Liberals shall rule instead."
		clr_country_flag = political_showdown
		set_country_flag = election_overridden
		ruling_party_ideology = liberal
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				location = { is_colonial = no }
				is_primary_culture = yes
				fascist = 20
			}
			ideology = {
				value = fascist
				factor = 0.10
			}
			militancy = 6
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				location = { is_colonial = no }
			}
			militancy = 2
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = { liberal = 20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5

country_event = {
	id = 99380015
	title = "Assassination Attempt!"
	desc = "An assassin has struck at our monarch while he was on his whistle-stop tour!"
	picture = "ferdinand"
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		has_country_modifier = tour 
		any_state = {
			is_colonial = no
			average_militancy = 5
		}
		NOT = {	has_country_modifier = national_instability }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 150
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			war = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			NOT = { average_militancy = 2 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { average_militancy = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			any_state = {
				is_colonial = no
				average_militancy = 6
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			any_state = {
				is_colonial = no
				average_militancy = 7
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			any_owned_province = {
				is_colonial = no
				controlled_by = REB
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Ye Gads!"
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						is_greater_power = yes
						is_secondary_power = yes
					}
				}
			}
			owner = { prestige = -10 }
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { 
					is_greater_power = no
					is_secondary_power = no
				}
			}
			owner = { prestige = -5 }
		}
		remove_country_modifier = tour
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = national_instability
			duration = 365
		}
	}
}

		}

			OR = {
				is_primary_culture = yes

	trigger = {	exists = yes
		ai = yes
		war = no
		is_culture_group = germanic
		state_n_government = 1
		OR = {
			capital = 549
			capital = 619
		}
		any_greater_power = {
			ai = yes
			is_culture_group = germanic
			NOT = { capital = 549 }
			NOT = { capital = 619 }
			OR = {
				alliance_with = THIS
				relation = { who = THIS value = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Unacceptable!"
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				is_greater_power = yes
				is_culture_group = germanic
				NOT = { capital = 549 }
				NOT = { capital = 619 }
				OR = {
					alliance_with = THIS
					relation = { who = THIS value = 0 }
				}
			}
			leave_alliance = THIS
			relation = { who = THIS value = -100 }
			add_casus_belli = {
				target = THIS
				type = humiliate
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}
}

#Forming Germany as Austria

#This event fires if Austria or Austria-Hungary is in a position to form Germany
#but still owns non-Austrian/German core provinces

country_event = {
	id = 31510
	title = "EVTNAME31510" #A Greater Austrian Destiny?
	desc = "EVTDESC31510"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC31510_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC31510_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC31510_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "threehurrahs"
	major = yes
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		OR = {
			tag = AUS
			tag = KUK
		}
		prestige = 45
		state_n_government = 1
		is_greater_power = yes
		war = no
		GER = {
			all_core = {
				OR = {
					owned_by = THIS
					owner = {
						in_sphere = THIS
						OR = {
							is_vassal = no
							vassal_of = THIS
						}
						war = no
						is_greater_power = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
		any_owned_province = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					is_core = AUS
					is_core = GER
					is_colonial = yes
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			exists = GER
			has_country_flag = austrian_destiny
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "We will give up nothing to form Germany."
		set_country_flag = austrian_destiny
		set_country_flag = austrian_greater_germany
		badboy = 40
		all_core = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_core = HUN }
			}
			add_core = GER
		}
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core = HUN
					is_core = POL
					is_core = ROM
					is_core = CRO
					is_core = VEN
					is_core = LOM
					is_core = SER
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = nationalist_agitation
				duration = 1095
			}
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				is_primary_culture = no
				is_accepted_culture = no
			}
			consciousness = 5
			militancy = 5
			ideology = {
				value = separatist
				factor = 0.4
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				is_greater_power = yes
				capital_scope = { continent = europe }
			}
			leave_alliance = THIS
			relation = { who = THIS value = -100 }
			casus_belli = {
				target = THIS
				type = free_peoples
				months = 60
			}
			casus_belli = {
				target = SGF
				type = free_peoples
				months = 60
			}
			casus_belli = {
				target = GER
				type = free_peoples
				months = 60
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Give limited autonomy to our non-German states."
		set_country_flag = austrian_destiny
		set_country_flag = austrian_greater_germany
		badboy = 20
		all_core = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_core = HUN }
			}
			add_core = GER
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				is_primary_culture = no
				is_accepted_culture = no
				location = { is_core = GER }
			}
			consciousness = 5
			militancy = 5
			ideology = {
				value = separatist
				factor = 0.4
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_culture_group = germanic }
				NOT = { tag = HUN }
				any_core = {
					owned_by = THIS
					NOT = { is_core = GER }
					is_colonial = no
				}
				exists = no
				is_cultural_union = no
			}
			country_event = 31511
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = HUN
				any_core = {
					owned_by = THIS
					NOT = { is_core = GER }
					is_colonial = no
				}
				exists = no
				is_cultural_union = no
			}
			country_event = 31511
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				is_greater_power = yes
				capital_scope = { continent = europe }
			}
			relation = { who = THIS value = -50 }
			casus_belli = {
				target = THIS
				type = release_puppet
				months = 60
			}
			casus_belli = {
				target = SGF
				type = release_puppet
				months = 60
			}
			casus_belli = {
				target = GER
				type = release_puppet
				months = 60
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				badboy = 0.2
				NOT = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
				NOT = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				tag = KUK
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				government = absolute_monarchy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					government = democracy
					government = hms_government
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Give independence to our non-German states."
		set_country_flag = austrian_destiny
		set_country_flag = austrian_greater_germany
		badboy = 10
		all_core = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_core = HUN }
			}
			add_core = GER
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				is_primary_culture = no
				is_accepted_culture = no
				location = { is_core = GER }
			}
			consciousness = 5
			militancy = 5
			ideology = {
				value = separatist
				factor = 0.4
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_culture_group = germanic }
				NOT = { tag = HUN }
				any_core = {
					owned_by = THIS
					NOT = { is_core = GER }
					is_colonial = no
				}
				exists = no
				is_cultural_union = no
			}
			country_event = 31512
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = HUN
				any_core = {
					owned_by = THIS
					NOT = { is_core = GER }
					is_colonial = no
				}
				exists = no
				is_cultural_union = no
			}
			country_event = 31512
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				is_greater_power = yes
				capital_scope = { continent = europe }
			}
			relation = { who = THIS value = -50 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				war_policy = jingoism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { badboy = 0.2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = KUK
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				government = absolute_monarchy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					government = democracy
					government = hms_government
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "$COUNTRY$ has no interest in becoming Germany."
		set_country_flag = austrian_destiny
		prestige = -25
		badboy = -5
		any_pop = {
			limit = { is_culture_group = germanic }
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = jingoism
				factor = 8
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = pacifism
				factor = -4
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				tag = KUK
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					government = proletarian_dictatorship
					government = fascist_dictatorship
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 31511
	title = "EVTNAME31511" #Limited Autonomy
	desc = "EVTDESC31511"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Excellent!"
		FROM = {
			any_owned = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core = GER }
					is_core = THIS
				}
				secede_province = THIS
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			prestige = -5
			create_vassal = THIS
			diplomatic_influence = {
				who = THIS
				value = 200
			}
			relation = {
				who = THIS
				value = 100
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				is_greater_power = yes
				OR = {
					neighbour = THIS
					is_culture_group = THIS
					tag = FRA
					tag = RUS
					tag = ENG
				}
			}
			diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = 100 }
		}
		prestige = -100
		any_pop = {
			limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }
			consciousness = 4
			militancy = 4
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = { is_culture_group = germanic }
			militancy = -4
		}
	}
}

#Austria Joining Germany

#This fires if Austria or Austria-Hungary is in Germany's sphere
#but still own non-Austrian/German core provinces
#this is also triggered if they're in sphere at the time of Germany's formation

country_event = {
	id = 31515
	title = "EVTNAME31515" #The Greater Germany Question
	desc = "EVTDESC31515"
	major = yes
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		OR = {
			tag = AUS
			tag = KUK
		}
		is_greater_power = no
		war = no
		ai = yes
		GER = {
			war = no
			exists = yes
			is_sphere_leader_of = THIS
		}
		any_owned_province = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					is_core = AUS
					is_core = GER
					is_colonial = yes
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			is_vassal = no
			vassal_of = GER
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = austrian_destiny }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "We will join Greater Germany, no matter what."
		set_country_flag = wants_to_unify
		set_country_flag = austrian_destiny
		GER = { country_event = 31516 }
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				is_primary_culture = no
				is_accepted_culture = no
			}
			consciousness = 6
			militancy = 6
			ideology = {
				value = separatist
				factor = 0.4
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				is_secondary_power = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = KUK
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					government = democracy
					government = hms_government
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					government = absolute_monarchy
					government = prussian_constitutionalism
					government = hms_government
				}
				GER = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							government = absolute_monarchy
							government = prussian_constitutionalism
							government = hms_government
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				government = proletarian_dictatorship
				GER = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				government = proletarian_dictatorship
				GER = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				government = fascist_dictatorship
				GER = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				government = fascist_dictatorship
				GER = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "We shall give our non-German states independence before joining Germany."
		set_country_flag = wants_to_unify
		set_country_flag = austrian_destiny
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				is_primary_culture = no
				is_accepted_culture = no
				location = { NOT = { is_core = THIS } }
			}
			consciousness = 3
			militancy = 3
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				is_primary_culture = no
				is_accepted_culture = no
				location = { is_core = THIS }
			}
			consciousness = 5
			militancy = 5
			ideology = {
				value = separatist
				factor = 0.4
			}
		}
		GER = { country_event = 31519 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				is_secondary_power = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				tag = KUK
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					government = absolute_monarchy
					government = prussian_constitutionalism
					government = hms_government
				}
				GER = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							government = absolute_monarchy
							government = prussian_constitutionalism
							government = hms_government
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					government = democracy
					government = hms_government
				}
				GER = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							government = democracy
							government = hms_government
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					government = proletarian_dictatorship
					government = fascist_dictatorship					
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					government = presidential_dictatorship
					government = bourgeois_dictatorship
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				government = proletarian_dictatorship
				GER = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				government = fascist_dictatorship
				GER = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Our path does not lie with Germany."
		clr_country_flag = wants_to_unify
		set_country_flag = austrian_destiny
		GER = { country_event = 31518 }
		prestige = -10
		badboy = -5
		any_pop = {
			limit = { is_culture_group = germanic }
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = jingoism
				factor = 8
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = pacifism
				factor = -4
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				tag = KUK
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				government = proletarian_dictatorship
				GER = { NOT = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				government = fascist_dictatorship
				GER = { NOT = { government = fascist_dictatorship } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
					government = presidential_dictatorship
					government = bourgeois_dictatorship
				}
				GER = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							government = presidential_dictatorship
							government = bourgeois_dictatorship
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
					government = democracy
					government = hms_government
				}
				GER = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							government = democracy
							government = hms_government
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
					government = absolute_monarchy
					government = prussian_constitutionalism
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#triggered for Germany if Austria declares its intentions to join no matter what

country_event = {
	id = 31516
	title = "EVTNAME31516" #Austria Petitions to Join Germany
	desc = "EVTDESC31516"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC31531_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC31531_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC31531_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "threehurrahs"
	major = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Greater Germany, all of it, is our destiny."
		badboy = 40
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = KUK
				tag = FROM
			}
			all_core = {
				limit = { is_core = HUN }
				remove_core = KUK
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			all_core = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core = HUN }
				}
				add_core = GER
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = KUK
				tag = FROM
			}
			all_core = { add_core = AUS }
		}
		inherit = FROM
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				is_greater_power = yes
				capital_scope = { continent = europe }
			}
			leave_alliance = THIS
			relation = { who = THIS value = -100 }
			casus_belli = {
				target = THIS
				type = free_peoples
				months = 60
			}
		}
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core = HUN
					is_core = POL
					is_core = ROM
					is_core = CRO
					is_core = VEN
					is_core = LOM
					is_core = SER
				}
			}
			any_pop = {
				limit = {
					is_primary_culture = no
					is_accepted_culture = no
				}
				militancy = 4
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = nationalist_agitation
				duration = 1095
			}
		}			
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "$FROMCOUNTRY$'s non-German states will first have independence."
		badboy = 20
		FROM = {
			all_core = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core = HUN }
				}
				add_core = GER
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				is_greater_power = yes
				capital_scope = { continent = europe }
			}
			relation = { who = THIS value = -50 }
		}
		FROM = { country_event = 31520 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					government = presidential_dictatorship
					government = bourgeois_dictatorship
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					government = democracy
					government = hms_government
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				badboy = 0.2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Such a union is too risky."
		FROM = { clr_country_flag = wants_to_unify }
		prestige = -25
		badboy = -5
		relation = { who = FROM value = -50 }
		any_pop = {
			limit = { is_culture_group = germanic }
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = jingoism
				factor = 8
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = pacifism
				factor = -4
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				war_policy = jingoism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					war_policy = anti_military
					war_policy = pacifism
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					government = proletarian_dictatorship
					government = fascist_dictatorship
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 31517
	title = "Independence From $FROMCOUNTRY$!"
	desc = "We have been granted independence from $FROMCOUNTRY$!"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Excellent!"
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = AUS
					tag = KUK
				}
				exists = yes
			}
			any_owned = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core = GER }
					is_core = THIS
				}
				secede_province = THIS
			}
		}
		GER = {
			any_owned = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core = GER }
					is_core = THIS
				}
				secede_province = THIS
			}
			prestige = -5
			diplomatic_influence = {
				who = THIS
				value = 200
			}
			relation = {
				who = THIS
				value = 100
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				is_greater_power = yes
				OR = {
					neighbour = THIS
					is_culture_group = THIS
					tag = FRA
					tag = RUS
					tag = ENG
				}
			}
			diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = 100 }
		}
		prestige = -100
		any_pop = {
			limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }
			consciousness = -3
			militancy = -6
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = { is_culture_group = germanic }
			militancy = 4
		}
	}
}

#triggered if Austria/Austria-Hungary refuses to join Germany

country_event = {
	id = 31518
	title = "EVTNAME31518" #Austria Refuses German Unity!
	desc = "EVTDESC31518"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC31518_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC31518_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC31518_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "threehurrahs"
	major = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Greater Germany is our destiny."
		badboy = 20
		diplomatic_influence = { who = FROM value = -400 }
		relation = { who = FROM value = -400 }
		FROM = {
			all_core = {
				limit = {
					culture = north_german
					NOT = { is_core = HUN }
				}
				add_core = GER
			}
		}
		add_casus_belli = {
			target = FROM
			type = humiliate
			months = 60
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				is_greater_power = yes
				capital_scope = { continent = europe }
			}
			leave_alliance = THIS
			relation = { who = THIS value = -200 }
			casus_belli = {
				target = THIS
				type = cut_down_to_size
				months = 60
			}
			casus_belli = {
				target = THIS
				type = free_peoples
				months = 60
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
					government = presidential_dictatorship
					government = bourgeois_dictatorship
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					government = democracy
					government = hms_government
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				badboy = 0.2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "We will accept the $FROMCOUNTRY_ADJ$ decision."
		prestige = -25
		badboy = -5
		relation = { who = FROM value = 50 }
		any_pop = {
			limit = { is_culture_group = germanic }
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = jingoism
				factor = 8
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = pacifism
				factor = -4
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				war_policy = jingoism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
					war_policy = anti_military
					war_policy = pacifism
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					government = proletarian_dictatorship
					government = fascist_dictatorship
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					government = presidential_dictatorship
					government = bourgeois_dictatorship
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = 31520 }
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				is_greater_power = yes
				capital_scope = { continent = europe }
			}

				target = THIS
				type = free_peoples
				months = 60
			}

				target = THIS
				type = cut_down_to_size
				months = 60
			}
		}

			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0

					government = proletarian_dictatorship
					government = fascist_dictatorship
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					government = presidential_dictatorship
					government = bourgeois_dictatorship
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				badboy = 0.2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {

		prestige = -25
		badboy = -5
		relation = { who = FROM value = -50 }

				issue = jingoism
				factor = 8
			}

				issue = pacifism

			}
		}

			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				war_policy = jingoism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					war_policy = anti_military
					war_policy = pacifism
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					government = democracy
					government = hms_government
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 31520
	title = "Unification with Germany"
	desc = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ has accepted our proposal."
	news = yes
	news_title = "EVTNAME31520_NEWS_TITLE"
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC31520_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC31520_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC31520_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "threehurrahs"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Excellent!"
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { tag = KUK }
			}
			owner = {
				all_core = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core = HUN } }
					add_core = AUS
				}
				all_core = { remove_core = KUK }
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_culture_group = germanic }
				NOT = { tag = HUN }
				any_core = {
					owned_by = THIS
					NOT = { is_core = GER }
					is_colonial = no
				}
				exists = no
				is_cultural_union = no
			}
			country_event = 31517
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = HUN
				any_core = {
					owned_by = THIS
					NOT = { is_core = GER }
					is_colonial = no
				}
				exists = no
				is_cultural_union = no
			}
			country_event = 31517
		}
		GER = { inherit = THIS }
	}
}

#triggered if Austria or Austria-Hungary no longer owns Austria proper

country_event = {
	id = 31521
	title = "EVTNAME31521" #Dissolution of Austria
	desc = "EVTDESC31521"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC31521_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC31521_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC31521_NEWS_SHORT"
	major = yes
	picture = "unite"
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		OR = {
			tag = AUS
			tag = KUK
		}
		ai = yes
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = austria_dissolved
			owns = 619
			owns = 612
			owns = 616
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Oh no!"
		set_country_flag = austria_dissolved
		prestige = -25
		all_core = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					region = AUS_619
					region = AUS_612
					region = AUS_613
					region = AUS_734
				}
			}
			remove_core = THIS
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { tag = KUK }
			}
			owner = {
				all_core = {
					add_core = AUS
					remove_core = KUK
				}
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { vassal_of = THIS }
			leave_alliance = THIS
			country_event = 31523
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				neighbour = THIS
				exists = yes
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
			}
			country_event = 31522
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
				exists = no
				is_cultural_union = no
			}
			country_event = 31526
		}
	}
}

#This fires if Austria is in Germany's sphere
#and does not own non-Austrian/German core provinces
#this is also triggered if they're in sphere at the time of Germany's formation

country_event = {
	id = 31530
	title = "EVTNAME31515" #The Greater Germany Question
	desc = "EVTDESC31530"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
		tag = AUS
		is_greater_power = no
		war = no
		GER = {
			war = no
			exists = yes
			is_sphere_leader_of = THIS
		}
		NOT = {
			any_owned_province = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						is_core = AUS
						is_core = GER
						is_colonial = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			is_vassal = no
			vassal_of = GER
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = austrian_destiny }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "We will petition to join Germany."
		set_country_flag = wants_to_unify
		set_country_flag = austrian_destiny
		GER = { country_event = 31531 }
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				is_primary_culture = no
				is_accepted_culture = no
			}
			consciousness = 6
			militancy = 6
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				is_secondary_power = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					alliance_with = GER
					relation = { who = GER value = 100 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				government = proletarian_dictatorship
				GER = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				government = proletarian_dictatorship
				GER = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				government = fascist_dictatorship
				GER = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				government = fascist_dictatorship
				GER = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Our path does not lie with Germany."
		clr_country_flag = wants_to_unify
		set_country_flag = austrian_destiny
		GER = { country_event = 31518 }
		prestige = -10
		badboy = -5
		any_pop = {
			limit = { is_culture_group = germanic }
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = jingoism
				factor = 8
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = pacifism
				factor = -4
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				is_secondary_power = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				truce_with = GER
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = {
					relation = { who = GER value = 0 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				government = fascist_dictatorship
				GER = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				government = proletarian_dictatorship
				GER = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				OR = {
					government = democracy
					government = prussian_constitutionalism
					government = hms_government
				}
				GER = {
					OR = {
						government = democracy
						government = prussian_constitutionalism
						government = hms_government
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = 31531
	title = "EVTNAME31516" #Austria Petitions to Join Germany
	desc = "EVTDESC31531"

	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC31531_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC31531_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC31531_NEWS_SHORT"

	major = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Greater Germany is our destiny."
		badboy = 10
		FROM = {
			all_core = { add_core = GER }
		}
		inherit = FROM
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				is_greater_power = yes
				capital_scope = { continent = europe }
				OR = {
					tag = FRA
					tag = RUS
					NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
				}
			}
			leave_alliance = THIS
			relation = { who = THIS value = -50 }
			casus_belli = {
				target = THIS
				type = cut_down_to_size
				months = 60
			}
		}			
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				badboy = 0.6
				NOT = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
				NOT = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Such a union is too risky."
		FROM = { clr_country_flag = wants_to_unify }
		prestige = -25
		badboy = -5
		relation = { who = FROM value = -50 }
		any_pop = {
			limit = { is_culture_group = germanic }
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = jingoism
				factor = 8
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				issue = pacifism
				factor = -4
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

		tag = FRA
		412 = { NOT = { owned_by = THIS } }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = boulanger_director }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen =  {
		months = 2
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = boulanger_director
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVT99937OPTA"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = war_minister_boulanger
			duration = 7300
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = french_revanchism
			duration = -1
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				is_primary_culture = yes
				is_accepted_culture = yes
				OR = {
					type = soldiers
					type = officers
				}
			}
			ideology = { factor = 0.2 value = conservative }
			ideology = { factor = 0.1 value = reactionary }
			dominant_issue = { factor = 0.20 value = jingoism }
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				strata = poor
				is_culture_group = french
				location = { is_core = THIS }
			}
			ideology = { factor = 0.1 value = conservative }
			ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = liberal }
			dominant_issue = { factor = 0.10 value = jingoism }
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				location = { is_core = THIS }
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				ideology = reactionary
				factor = -4
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				ideology = conservative
				factor = -2
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	title = "EVTNAME95655" #The Unequal Treaty
	desc = "EVTDESC95655"
	picture = "Opiumwar"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Give them what they want."
		FRA = { country_event = 95656 }
		prestige = -10
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_country_modifier = uncivilized_isolationism }
			}
			owner = {
				remove_country_modifier = uncivilized_isolationism
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "western_influences"
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { diplomatic_reform = isolationism }
			}
			owner = {
				economic_reform = interactive
				activate_technology = classicism_n_early_romanticism
				any_pop = {
					scaled_militancy = {
						ideology = liberal
						factor = -10
					}
					scaled_militancy = {
						ideology = conservative
						factor = 3
					}
					scaled_militancy = {
						ideology = reactionary
						factor = 6
					}
				}
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { owns = 1380 }
					owns = 1375
				}
			}
			owner = {
				any_owned = {
					limit = { region = DAI_1375 }
					secede_province = FRA
				}
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = { owns = 1380 }
			}
			owner = {
				any_owned = {
					limit = { region = DAI_1380 }
					secede_province = FRA
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}

			factor = 0
		}
	}
